 Today, World Thalassemia Day is being celebrated all over the world
 thilacemia bacchon ko unke mata-pita se milane vaala anuvaanshik rakt rog he
 This disease is recognized in the child only after 3 months
 zyaadaatar bacchon main dekhi jane vaali is beemaari kii vajah se sharir main rakt kii kami hone lagati he or uchit upachaar na milane par bachche kii mrityu tak ho sakati he
 Let's know what is this disease and its symptoms and methods of prevention
 kya he yah beemaari-aamtaur par har saamaanya vyakti ke sharir main laal rakt kanon kii umr kareeb 120 dinon kii hoti he, lekin thilacemia se peedit rogi ke sharir main laal rakt kanon kii umr ghatakar maatr 20 din hi rah jaati he
 It directly affects the hemoglobin of the person
 jiske kam hone par vyakti anemia kaa shikaar ho jaataa he or har samay kisi na kisi beemaari se grasit rahane lagata he
 Types of Thalassemia - Thalassemia is of two types
 miner thilacemia yaa major thilacemia
 When a chromosome is present in the body of a woman or a male, the child becomes a victim of minor thalassemia
 lekin agar mahila or purush donon vyaktiyon ke chromosome kharaab ho jate hai to yah major thilacemia kii sthiti banaata he
 Due to which, after 6 months after the birth of the child, blood stops in his body and he needs to be given blood again and again
 thilacemia kii pahchaan-thilacemia asaamaanya haemoglobin or red blad cells ke utpaadan se judaa ek blad disorder he
 In this disease, due to reduced red blood cells in the patient's body, he becomes a victim of anemia
 jisaki vajah se use har samay kamajori,thakaavat mahasoos karnaa, pet main sujan, dark urine, twachaa kaa rang pilaa pad saktaa he
 Home Remedies to Avoid Thalassemia - To save the child from this serious disease, firstly, the boy and girl should have blood tests made mandatory before marriage
 - agar aapane khun kii jaanch karwaae bina hi shaadi kar lee he to garbhavastha ke 8 se 11 hafte ke bheetar hi apane diene kii jaanch karvaa leni chahie
 - a person suffering from minor thalassemia lives his life towards any normal person
 bina khun kii jaanch karwaae kai baar to use pataa hi nahin chalata ki uske khun main koi dosha bhi he
 In such a situation, if the blood of husband and wife is tested before marriage, then the child from this genetic disease can be saved to a great extent
 thilacemia kaa upachaar-thilacemia kaa ilaaj, rog kii gambhirtha par nirbhar karata he
 Many times children suffering from Thalassemia may need blood transfusions 2-3 times in a month
 -bone maro pratyaropan se in rog kaa ilaaj safaltaapurvak sambhav he lekin bone maro kaa milan ek behad mushkil prakriya he
 In addition, this serious disease can also be treated by blood transfusions, bone marrow transplants, medications and supplements, surgery to remove the possible spleen or gallbladder
